     1	# Inter-Project Communication Specification
     2	
     3	**Created**: 2026-04-17
     4	**Owner**: Portfolio level (D:\Projects\)
     5	**Purpose**: Enable AI agents working on different projects to exchange requirements, deliverables, status updates, and confirmations without losing context across sessions.
     6	
     7	---
     8	
     9	## Problem
    10	
    11	Projects in the portfolio have dependencies (SMSS → WhoAMI, Literature System → WhoAMI, etc.). When an agent works on Project A, it may produce deliverables or need information from Project B. But:
    12	
    13	1. Agents working on different projects don't share context
    14	2. Information communicated verbally (in chat) is lost on session end
    15	3. Cross-project requirements discovered in one session may not reach the other project's agent
    16	
    17	## Solution: File-Based Inbox/Outbox
    18	
    19	Each project maintains two directories:
    20	
    21	```
    22	project_root/
    23	├── inbox/       ← messages addressed TO this project
    24	├── outbox/      ← messages sent FROM this project
    25	└── ...
    26	```
    27	
    28	### Message Lifecycle
    29	
    30	```
    31	Sender Agent                              Recipient Agent
    32	    │                                          │
    33	    ├─ writes message to own outbox/           │
    34	    ├─ copies same file to recipient inbox/    │
    35	    │                                          │
    36	    │  ─── session boundary ───                │
    37	    │                                          │
    38	    │                      recipient reads inbox/─┤
    39	    │                      marks status: read   ─┤
    40	    │                      acts on content      ─┤
    41	    │                      marks status: actioned─┤
    42	    │                      (optional: sends reply)│
    43	```
    44	
    45	### Message Format
    46	
    47	**Filename**: `YYYY-MM-DD-from-[source]-[topic-slug].md`
    48	
    49	**Header** (YAML frontmatter):
    50	```yaml
    51	---
    52	from: [source project name]
    53	to: [target project name]
    54	date: YYYY-MM-DD
    55	subject: [one-line subject]
    56	status: unread | read | actioned
    57	in-reply-to: [original filename, if reply]
    58	---
    59	```
    60	
    61	**Body**: Free-form markdown. Use tables, checklists, code blocks as appropriate.
    62	
    63	### Rules
    64	
    65	1. **Immutable received messages** — never edit a file in your inbox (mark status only). If you need to respond, write a new message.
    66	2. **Status field** — sender sets `unread`. Recipient changes to `read` after reading, `actioned` after completing any required action.
    67	3. **Archival** — messages with `status: actioned` older than 30 days → move to `inbox/_archive/`.
    68	4. **Registration** — register `inbox/` and `outbox/` in FILE_INDEX.md (one line each).
    69	5. **Session start check** — agents SHOULD scan inbox/ for `status: unread` messages at the start of each session, as part of the Recovery Chain.
    70	
    71	### Integration with Doc Harness
    72	
    73	**CURRENT_STATUS.md** — when a message requires action, add it to the Headlights (Next Steps):
    74	```markdown
    75	### Next Steps
    76	- [ ] Respond to WhoAMI request (inbox/2026-04-16-from-whoami-requirements.md)
    77	```
    78	
    79	**CLAUDE.md** — add inbox/outbox to the Recovery Chain:
    80	```markdown
    81	## Recovery Chain
    82	1. Read CLAUDE.md
    83	2. Read CURRENT_STATUS.md
    84	3. **Check inbox/ for unread messages**
    85	4. ...
    86	```
    87	
    88	**FILE_INDEX.md** — register:
    89	```markdown
    90	## Inter-Project Communication
    91	- `inbox/` — incoming messages from other projects
    92	- `outbox/` — sent messages to other projects
    93	- Reference: `D:\Projects\docs\INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC.md`
    94	```
    95	
    96	---
    97	
    98	## Required Iron Rule for Participating Projects
    99	
   100	**Every project that uses inbox/outbox MUST include the following iron rule in its own `CLAUDE.md`** (or equivalent project-entry document). This ensures future agents — even those joining the project long after setup — understand and comply with the mechanism.
   101	
   102	Copy the block below verbatim into your `CLAUDE.md` under "Project-Level Iron Rules" (or equivalent section). Adjust only the SMSS-specific examples if your project has different outbound-reference concerns.
   103	
   104	---
   105	
   106	```markdown
   107	**项目间通讯走 inbox/outbox 文件协议**（File-based inter-project communication）
   108	
   109	- **机制**：每个项目维护 `inbox/`（收信）和 `outbox/`（发信）两个目录。发送方写入自己的 `outbox/` 并复制到接收方的 `inbox/`。消息是 YAML frontmatter + Markdown body 的 `.md` 文件，文件名格式 `YYYY-MM-DD-from-[source]-[topic].md`。
   110	- **为什么必须走这个机制**：跨项目的 agent 不共享上下文；聊天中口述的信息会在会话结束时丢失；跨项目的需求/交付/确认必须以文件形式落盘才能被对方 agent 的 Recovery Chain 拾取。
   111	- **接收流程**（会话开始时 Recovery Chain 应检查 `inbox/`）：读 `status: unread` 的消息 → 标记 `status: read` → 执行动作后标记 `status: actioned`。永不修改收到的消息（append-only，需回复就写新消息）。
   112	- **发送流程**：写入自己的 `outbox/`（保留底稿）→ 复制同一文件到接收方的 `inbox/` → 在本项目的 CURRENT_STATUS（或等价状态文档）记录该次通讯（保证下次会话能追溯）。
   113	- **不走这个机制的后果**：本项目的内部文件（设计 spec、benchmark、内部数据）**不应被其他项目直接读取**。对外引用的数字、状态、交付物，必须通过 inbox 发送**确认快照**——这样既避免本项目内部重构破坏对方的引用，也避免对方引用过时或未经确认的数据。
   114	- **权威协议文档**：`D:\Projects\docs\INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC.md`（portfolio 级，含完整 lifecycle、Doc Harness 集成、依赖图、Quick Start、消息格式规范）
   115	- **Recovery Chain 集成**：CLAUDE.md 的 Recovery Chain 必须包含 "Check `inbox/` for unread messages"（通常作为第 2 步，紧跟在读入口文档之后）。
   116	- **FILE_INDEX 注册**：`inbox/` 和 `outbox/` 必须在 FILE_INDEX 中登记。
   117	```
   118	
   119	---
   120	
   121	## Current Projects
   122	
   123	| Project | inbox | outbox |
   124	|---------|-------|--------|
   125	| **Portfolio** (D:\Projects\) | N/A (coordination level) | N/A |

   151	### llm-hub 作为基础设施枢纽
   152	
   153	`llm-hub` 是继 `doc-harness` / `literature-search` 之后的第三个基础设施项目，负责**集中管理所有 LLM（在线 API + 本地部署 + 嵌入模型）**。
   154	
   155	所有涉及 LLM 访问的项目应通过 `from llm_hub import get_provider` 方式消费，而不是自行持有 API Key。llm-hub 一旦发生预设变更 / API 可用性变化 / 定价调整 / quirks 更新，应主动向 `lit-system-api` / `WhoAMI` 等已知消费者的 inbox 发送通知快照。
   156	
   157	## For New Project Agents: Quick Start
   158	
   159	When your project's CLAUDE.md mentions inter-project communication:
   160	
   161	1. Check if `inbox/` exists in your project root. If not, create it.
   162	2. Read any `status: unread` files in inbox/
   163	3. Mark them `status: read` after reading
   164	4. Act on any requirements, then mark `status: actioned`
   165	5. To send a message: write to your `outbox/` AND copy to the recipient's `inbox/`
   166	6. Full spec: this document (`D:\Projects\docs\INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC.md`)

    59	## Project Overview
    60	
    61	Prepare a complete, competitive academic job market package for a Finance PhD (market microstructure, computational equilibrium methods) targeting Beijing universities and research institutions. The candidate has exceptional technical depth and research scale but zero publications, zero conference presentations, and zero teaching experience — requiring both a standard materials package and innovative differentiation strategies.
    62

    64	- **Standard package**: CV, Research Statement, Teaching Statement, Cover Letters, Dissertation Abstract, Technical Portfolio — all present and up-to-date

    66	- **Narrative**: "An engineer-scholar who builds research infrastructure, not just papers"
    67	
    68	## Project-Level Iron Rules
    69	
    70	- All materials must be based on confirmed facts only — no fabricated achievements
    71	- Every number must match the current thesis state (291 pages, 147 references, 10 models)
    72	- Advisor information not displayed until explicitly authorized
    73	- Recommenders left as "Available upon request" until confirmed
    74	- Narrative coherence: every material reinforces the same positioning
    75	- **深入优先于完成**：不要急于"做完一个阶段"然后总结庆祝。一份真正写好的材料胜过十份走过场的材料。当你觉得"差不多了可以收尾了"的时候，问自己：这份东西拿给一个严肃的招聘委员会成员看，哪里会让他皱眉？去修那里，而不是去写总结。
    76	- **项目间通讯走 inbox/outbox 文件协议**（File-based inter-project communication）
    77	  - **机制**：每个项目维护 `inbox/`（收信）和 `outbox/`（发信）两个目录。发送方写入自己的 `outbox/` 并复制到接收方的 `inbox/`。消息是 YAML frontmatter + Markdown body 的 `.md` 文件，文件名格式 `YYYY-MM-DD-from-[source]-[topic].md`。
    78	  - **为什么必须走这个机制**：跨项目的 agent 不共享上下文；聊天中口述的信息会在会话结束时丢失；跨项目的需求/交付/确认必须以文件形式落盘才能被对方 agent 的 Recovery Chain 拾取。
    79	  - **接收流程**（会话开始时 Recovery Chain 应检查 `inbox/`）：读 `status: unread` 的消息 → 标记 `status: read` → 执行动作后标记 `status: actioned`。永不修改收到的消息（append-only，需回复就写新消息）。
    80	  - **发送流程**：写入自己的 `outbox/`（保留底稿）→ 复制同一文件到接收方的 `inbox/` → 在 CURRENT_STATUS 记录该次通讯。
    81	  - **不走这个机制的后果**：本项目的内部文件不应被其他项目直接读取；对外引用的数字/状态/交付物必须通过 inbox 发送**确认快照**。
    82	  - **权威协议文档**：`D:\Projects\docs\INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC.md`
    83	  - **FILE_INDEX 注册**：`inbox/` 和 `outbox/` 已登记。
    84	- **状态文档维护必须局部编辑（default）**：
    85	  - `CURRENT_STATUS.md`：仅更新受影响小节（Tire Tracks / Car Body / Headlights / Driving Manual），禁止无必要整文重写。
    86	  - `WORKLOG.md`：append-only，只新增 phase/补充勘误/更新 TOC；禁止改写既有 phase 正文。
    87	  - 只有在“明确 phase transition”或“结构模板修复”时允许整段迁移；且必须在 `WORKLOG` 记录原因与范围。
    88	
    89	## Key Technical Information
    90	
    91	- All materials are Markdown files (PDF output pipeline planned in Phase 3)
    92	- Chinese and English versions exist for: CV, Research Statement, Teaching Statement
    93	- Cover letter templates are modular with swappable paragraphs for different position types
    94	- Website: Next.js 16 + Tailwind CSS v4 + Framer Motion, code at `site/`
    95	- Design spec: `site/docs/superpowers/specs/2026-04-04-website-redesign-design.md`
    96	
    97	## Doc Harness — Operational Rules
    98	<!-- doc-harness-ops-version: 1.4.1 -->
    99	
   100	> Complete specification: see `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` in this directory.
   101	
   102	### Core Principle: "Write It Down or Lose It"
   103	
   104	Important information must be **written to a file** and **registered in FILE_INDEX**. Not written = lost. Not registered = undiscoverable = effectively lost.
   105	
   106	Registration scope in WhoAMI: register **agent-generated documents and key assets required by the Recovery Chain**, not every file in the repository.
   107	
   108	### Four Core Documents
   109	
   110	| Document | Role | When to update |
   111	|----------|------|---------------|
   112	| **CLAUDE.md** | Project entry | Phase transitions; one-line status every session end |
   113	| **CURRENT_STATUS.md** | Active status | Every session |
   114	| **FILE_INDEX.md** | File catalog by category | When files created/deleted |
   115	| **WORKLOG.md** | Complete history (append-only) | Phase transitions |
   116	
   117	### Session End Checklist
   118	
   119	- [ ] CURRENT_STATUS reflects all work?
   120	- [ ] Next steps accurate?
   121	- [ ] Dates refreshed?
   122	- [ ] New files registered in FILE_INDEX?
   123	- [ ] Anything unsaved? → Write it down!


</details>

<system>374 lines read from file starting from line 1000. Total lines in file: 1373. End of file reached. Lines [1370] were truncated.</system>
  1000	**FILE_INDEX.md** — register both directories under their own category:
  1001	
  1002	```markdown
  1003	## Inter-Project Communication
  1004	- `inbox/` — Incoming messages from other projects
  1005	- `outbox/` — Outgoing messages (drafts and sent-copies)
  1006	```
  1007	
  1008	**Recovery Chain (CLAUDE.md)** — add one task-conditional entry:
  1009	
  1010	```markdown
  1011	### Task-conditional
  1012	- If `inbox/` has any file with `status: unread`: read and action those first
  1013	- ...
  1014	```
  1015	
  1016	Note: this entry sits in **task-conditional**, not must-read. Reading the entire inbox at every session start would burn context; only unread messages matter. If inbox is empty or all messages are `read`/`actioned`, this entry is a no-op.
  1017	
  1018	### 14.6 Quick Start for a fresh agent
  1019	
  1020	If you arrive at a project and see `inbox/` and `outbox/` in the root, the project uses this protocol. Do this:
  1021	
  1022	1. Scan `inbox/` for any file whose frontmatter has `status: unread` (see §14.3 for the frontmatter schema and lifecycle vocabulary).
  1023	2. For each: read it, take the required action if any, update its `status` field (`read` after reading, `actioned` after completing).
  1024	3. Before modifying project internal files that other projects might reference (models, interfaces, numbers), consider whether a snapshot needs to be sent to dependents via their inbox.
  1025	4. To send: write to your project's `outbox/` AND copy the same file to the recipient's `inbox/` (same filename — see §14.3). Record the exchange in CURRENT_STATUS.
  1026	5. If you encounter an inbox file that looks wrong (no frontmatter, unknown status value, nonconforming filename), handle it per §14.8 rather than guessing.
  1027	
  1028	Everything you need is in this chapter. No external file required.
  1029	
  1030	### 14.7 Adopting on an existing project
  1031	
  1032	To retrofit an existing project:
  1033	1. Create `inbox/` and `outbox/` at project root.
  1034	2. Copy the iron rule block from §14.5 into CLAUDE.md's Iron Rules section.
  1035	3. Add the task-conditional entry to Recovery Chain (also §14.5).
  1036	4. Add the `## Inter-Project Communication` category to FILE_INDEX.
  1037	5. (Optional) Send a notification message to dependent projects that this project is now reachable via inbox.
  1038	
  1039	### 14.8 Malformed message handling
  1040	
  1041	When `inbox/` contains a file that does not conform to §14.3, do NOT silently skip it and do NOT guess. Apply the classification below, then act once — never enter a retry loop on a malformed file.
  1042	
  1043	| Symptom | Lenient or strict? | Action |
  1044	|---------|--------------------|--------|
  1045	| Filename does not match `YYYY-MM-DD-from-<source>-<topic>.md` but file has valid YAML | Lenient | Process normally. Note the filename anomaly in CURRENT_STATUS car body. Do NOT rename the file (it's the sender's record, immutable per §14.4 rule 1). |
  1046	| No YAML frontmatter at all | Strict | Move to `inbox/_malformed/` (create if missing). Write a one-line entry in CURRENT_STATUS car body: `#### Quarantined malformed inbox/<filename> (no YAML) on YYYY-MM-DD`. Do NOT attempt to parse the body. |
  1047	| YAML frontmatter present but `status:` field missing | Strict | Treat as `unread` for safety (err toward action). Add the `status: unread` line and proceed to read. Log the anomaly in car body. |
  1048	| `status:` has unknown value (not `unread`/`read`/`actioned`) | Strict | Treat as `unread`. Log the anomaly in car body. After reading, set to `read` (then `actioned` if applicable) using canonical values. |
  1049	| Required frontmatter field missing (`from`, `to`, `date`, `subject`) | Strict | Move to `inbox/_malformed/` with a one-line car body note. Do NOT fabricate the missing values. All four are required per §14.3. |
  1050	| `priority:` missing or has unknown value | Lenient | Treat as `priority: normal`. Log the anomaly in car body. |
  1051	| `in-reply-to:` missing entirely | Lenient | Treat as no-reply (null). No action needed. |
  1052	| Frontmatter references `in-reply-to:` pointing at a file that does not exist in this project's outbox | Lenient | Process normally; note the dangling reference in car body but do not block. |
  1053	| Multiple messages with the same filename (rare even after §14.3 disambiguator, e.g. two senders writing independently at the same moment) | Strict | The one on disk wins. Note in car body: `#### Filename collision observed on <name> — kept disk copy`. Do not merge contents. Report via `/doc-harness check` §1.7 so the sender can re-send with a different topic slug if needed. |
  1054	
  1055	`inbox/_malformed/` is not archival — it's a quarantine for agent/human inspection. Entries there should be reviewed by the user, not silently forgotten. `/doc-harness check` §1.7 reports the count.
  1056	
  1057	---
  1058	
  1059	## Appendix A: Phase Boundary Decision Guide
  1060	
  1061	| Signal | Transition? |
  1062	|--------|------------|
  1063	| Work goal fundamentally changes ("writing" → "reviewing") | ✅ Yes |
  1064	| User explicitly says "start something else" | ✅ Yes |
  1065	| Project pause >3 days | ✅ Yes (pause = phase end) |
  1066	| Car body exceeds 200 lines | ✅ Consider (signal, not hard rule) |
  1067	| Sub-task switch within same goal (Ch4→Ch5, both "literature reinforcement") | ❌ No — use sub-headings in car body |
  1068	| Temporary small task (fix a typo, then return) | ❌ No |
  1069	| Uncertain | ❌ Don't transition (avoid over-maintenance); use clear headings in car body |
  1070	
  1071	---
  1072	
  1073	## Appendix B: Quick Checklist
  1074	
  1075	Run through at session end:
  1076	
  1077	- [ ] CURRENT_STATUS "last updated" is today?
  1078	- [ ] All new files registered in FILE_INDEX?
  1079	- [ ] All work steps recorded in car body?
  1080	- [ ] Headlights "next steps" accurate?
  1081	- [ ] Any important information only in context? (Write it down!)
  1082	- [ ] If a phase transition happened: WORKLOG under ~1000 lines? (If over, trigger §5.5 archival.)
  1083	
  1084	---
  1085	
  1086	## Appendix C: Glossary
  1087	
  1088	| Term | Definition |
  1089	|------|-----------|
  1090	| **Project** | Basic unit of the Doc Harness system. A work stream with independent goals and outputs. |
  1091	| **Phase** | A period within a project with a clear goal. Transition triggers information flow operations. |
  1092	| **Leaf document** | Any file that is not one of the four core status documents. |
  1093	| **Car body / Tire tracks / Headlights / Driving manual** | Metaphors for the four sections of CURRENT_STATUS. |
  1094	| **Register** | Add a file to the appropriate category in FILE_INDEX. |
  1095	| **Write It Down** | First principle: important information must be saved to file and registered. |
  1096	| **SUPERSEDED** | Document has been replaced; marked at first line. |
  1097	| **Iron rule** | Project-level permanent rule defined in CLAUDE.md. |
  1098	
  1099	---

  1336	
  1337	## Appendix E: Design Choices (FAQ)
  1338	
  1339	### Why is inter-project inbox/outbox an optional mechanism, not a required one?
  1340	
  1341	Because many projects are standalone and have no dependents. Mandating inbox/outbox on every project would impose empty directories and an unused iron rule, eroding trust in the skill. The mechanism is offered as a standard optional feature with a complete self-contained spec (Chapter 14) so projects that need it can adopt it consistently and projects that don't need it ignore it.
  1342	
  1343	### Why is the mechanism described inside doc-harness instead of as a separate spec?
  1344	
  1345	Because an external spec is **brittle**. An agent working inside a project has no reliable entry point to an external file; over long project lifetimes the external reference tends to be lost, misinterpreted, or forgotten. By embedding the full mechanism into doc-harness's spec, every project that deploys `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` carries a self-contained description — the project becomes its own authoritative source for how the protocol works.
  1346	
  1347	### Why are PARKING_LOT.md and PHILOSOPHY.md optional, not mandatory?
  1348	
  1349	Not every project has deferred items or emergent cross-project principles worth recording. Mandating these files would produce empty shells that erode trust in the four-document system. Offer them as patterns; let each project adopt when there's content to put there.
  1350	
  1351	### Why keep must-read layer at 2–3 files?
  1352	
  1353	Any larger, and "must-read" becomes "should probably read," and agents start skipping entries or reading the whole project defensively. The two-layer split only works if the baseline is genuinely minimal. Entries that only apply to *some* work belong in task-conditional.
  1354	
  1355	### Why use line count (not phase count) as WORKLOG archival trigger?
  1356	
  1357	Phase density varies enormously across projects — from ~20 lines per phase (infrastructure work, terse records) to ~200 lines per phase (dense research work). Line count reflects the actual cost of reading the file, which is what we care about.
  1358	
  1359	---
  1360

  1372	| v1.4.1 | 2026-04-19 | **§5.5 WORKLOG archival correction — field feedback**: archive filename changed from quarterly bin `WORKLOG_ARCHIVE_<YYYY-QN>.md` to per-event date `WORKLOG_ARCHIVE_<YYYY-MM-DD>.md`. The quarterly scheme unbounded the archive for high-activity projects (a project writing 5,000 lines/quarter would put all 5,000 lines into one "archive" file, defeating the purpose). Per-event naming keeps each archive inherently bounded by the ~1000-line trigger. Cross-quarter-scar step (old rule 6) removed — no longer applicable. New rule 7: archival event must be recorded in CURRENT_STATUS car body so a next-session agent sees the history shift without diffing WORKLOG.      1	# Doc Harness — Entry Document
     2	
     3	**Last updated**: 2026-04-22
     4	**Current phase**: Phase 4 → Maintenance & field-feedback watch (⏳ active — kimi-skill created, Claude local install updated)
     5	**One-line status (as of 2026-04-22)**: v1.5.1 shipped — recall command added; token-efficiency rules enforced in search protocol; version numbers unified across all artifacts; PHILOSOPHY.md elevated to universal principles. Local installs (Claude + Kimi) and both repos synchronized.
     6	
     7	---
     8	
     9	## Recovery Chain
    10	
    11	### Must-read (baseline)
    12	
    13	1. This file (CLAUDE.md)
    14	2. `CURRENT_STATUS.md`
    15	
    16	### Task-conditional
    17	
    18	- If `inbox/` has any file with `status: unread`: read and action those first
    19	- If looking up a file: read `FILE_INDEX.md`
    20	- If investigating phase history: read `WORKLOG.md`
    21	- If editing the spec or operational rules: read `skill/spec.md` (authoritative)
    22	- If looking for principles forged by project practice: read `PHILOSOPHY.md`
    23	
    24	### Meta-rules
    25	
    26	- Self-contained: all entries point to project-internal files. No dependency on agent-side features.
    27	- Living: review at phase transitions.
    28	
    29	## Project Overview
    30	
    31	Doc Harness is a Claude Code skill that provides document-based project control for AI-human collaboration. It creates and maintains 5 status documents per project (CLAUDE.md, CURRENT_STATUS.md, FILE_INDEX.md, WORKLOG.md, DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md) that enable any agent or human to understand and resume project work purely from reading files.
    32	
    33	**Five commands**: `/doc-harness init` (create docs), `/doc-harness check` (audit + reflect), `/doc-harness sync` (repair drift), `/doc-harness flush` (emergency save), `/doc-harness recall` (retrieve information).
    34	
    35	**Core principle**: "Write It Down or Lose It" — context info is temporary, files are permanent.
    36	
    37	**Origin**: Designed and validated in `D:\Projects\project_reorganization\` (7 phases, 2026-04-01 ~ 04-03), then published as standalone skill.
    38	
    39	## Project-Level Iron Rules
    40	
    41	1. **中英文版本永远同步**: Every change to skill/ must be mirrored to skill-zh/, and vice versa. No exceptions.
    42	2. **Doc Harness adapts to project, not project to Doc Harness**: The skill must accommodate diverse project structures. Never impose rigid templates that break existing workflows.
    43	3. **spec.md is the authoritative specification**: All other files (operational_rules.md, init.md, check.md, README) derive from spec.md. Contradictions are resolved in favor of spec.md.
    44	4. **Test before release**: Every change must be validated (blind test, real project test, or simulation) before pushing to GitHub or updating installed copies.
    45	5. **Deployment sync**: After any change, update all 3 locations: dev source → GitHub push → installed copies (user-level + project-level).
    46	
    47	6. **Inter-project communication via inbox/outbox (file-based protocol)**
    48	
    49	   - **Mechanism**: This project maintains `inbox/` (received messages) and `outbox/` (sent messages). Messages are Markdown files with YAML frontmatter; filename `YYYY-MM-DD-from-<source>-<topic>.md`.
    50	   - **Why this is mandatory (if adopted)**: Cross-project information exchanged only in chat is lost on session end. File-based messages survive session boundaries and are discoverable by any future agent through this project's Recovery Chain.
    51	   - **Receiving**: Recovery Chain checks `inbox/` for `status: unread`. Read → update to `status: read`. After acting on the message → `status: actioned`. Never edit received messages beyond the status field; to respond, write a new message.
    52	   - **Sending**: Write to this project's `outbox/` (permanent sender-side record) AND copy the same file into the recipient project's `inbox/`. Record the exchange in CURRENT_STATUS so it is traceable next session.
    53	   - **Snapshots over pointers**: When communicating numbers/deliverables to another project, put the value in the message body rather than referencing internal files.
    54	   - **Full specification**: `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` §14 (in this project's root).
    55	
    56	## Key Technical Information
    57	
    58	**GitHub**: https://github.com/cilidinezy-commits/doc-harness (latest tag: v1.4)
    59	**License**: MIT
    60	
    61	**File structure**:
    62	```
    63	doc-harness/
    64	├── skill/           ← English skill files (5 files, authoritative)
    65	├── skill-zh/        ← Chinese skill files (5 files, synced)
    66	├── README.md        ← English project description
    67	├── README_zh.md     ← Chinese project description
    68	└── LICENSE          ← MIT
    69	```
    70	
    71	**Deployment locations** (installed copies must match dev source):
    72	- User-level: `~/.claude/skills/doc-harness/` ← from `skill/`
    73	- Project-level (ObsVault_Tools): `.claude/skills/doc-harness/` ← from `skill/`
    74	
    75	**Skill files** (same structure in both skill/ and skill-zh/):
    76	| File | Role |
    77	|------|------|
    78	| SKILL.md | Entry point + router |
    79	| init.md | `/doc-harness init` — create 5 docs |
    80	| check.md | `/doc-harness check` — audit + reflect |
    81	| operational_rules.md | Rules embedded in each project's CLAUDE.md (180 lines as of v1.4; delimited by `<!-- doc-harness-ops-start/end -->` sentinels) |
    82	| spec.md | Complete specification (1320 lines as of v1.4, 14 chapters + 5 appendices, TOC at top) |
    83	
    84	## Doc Harness — Operational Rules
    85	
    86	> Complete specification: see `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` in this directory.
    87	
    88	### Core Principle: "Write It Down or Lose It"
    89	
    90	Important information must be **written to a file** and **registered in FILE_INDEX**. Not written = lost. Not registered = undiscoverable = effectively lost.
    91	
    92	### Four Core Documents
    93	
    94	| Document | Role | When to update |
    95	|----------|------|---------------|
    96	| **CLAUDE.md** | Project entry | Phase transitions; one-line status every session end |
    97	| **CURRENT_STATUS.md** | Active status | Every session |
    98	| **FILE_INDEX.md** | File catalog by category | When files created/deleted |
    99	| **WORKLOG.md** | Complete history (append-only) | Phase transitions |
   100	
   101	### Session End Checklist
   102	
   103	- [ ] CURRENT_STATUS reflects all work?
   104	- [ ] Next steps accurate?
   105	- [ ] Dates refreshed?
   106	- [ ] New files registered in FILE_INDEX?
   107	- [ ] Anything unsaved? → Write it down!

     1	# Doc Harness — Init
     2	
     3	Create the five Doc Harness files for a new project.
     4	
     5	## Step 1: Gather Information
     6	
     7	You need these details. Gather from three sources in priority order:
     8	
     9	**Source A — Arguments**: Extract project name and description from `$ARGUMENTS`.
    10	**Source B — Context**: If the project was just discussed in conversation, extract goals, first tasks, constraints, technical details.
    11	**Source C — Ask the user**: For anything still unknown, ask explicitly. Do NOT guess. Reasonable inference from context is OK; fabrication is not.
    12	
    13	**Required** (must have before creating):
    14	- Project name (short, for document titles)
    15	- Project description (1-3 sentences)
    16	- First phase name (what is the initial work called)
    17	- First concrete task (what to do first — for "headlights")
    18	
    19	**Optional** (ask if unclear, OK to leave blank):
    20	- Initial iron rules
    21	- Key technical details (tools, languages, paths)
    22	- Known sub-projects
    23	- **Inter-project inbox/outbox**: one y/n question — "Does this project coordinate with other projects (has dependencies in either direction)? If yes, I'll enable the inter-project inbox/outbox protocol (Chapter 14 of the spec)." Default: **yes** if the user mentioned dependencies or sibling projects in context; **no** for standalone projects. If enabled, see Step 3.6 below.
    24	
    25	## Step 2: Check Existing Files and Project State
    26	
    27	Check the target directory for three situations:
    28	
    29	**(a) Clean directory** (no files, or only trivial starter files like a blank README/LICENSE) → proceed to Step 3 with blank templates.
    30	
    31	**(b) Doc Harness already present** (CLAUDE.md + CURRENT_STATUS.md + ... already exist) → do NOT overwrite. Warn the user and suggest `/doc-harness check` instead. If only *some* of the 5 files exist (partial or broken state), offer to complete the missing ones (mid-project adoption mode, see (c)) rather than wiping the partial state.
    32	
    33	**(c) Non-empty directory without Doc Harness** (has code, notes, existing README, accumulated files) → this is **mid-project adoption**. Do NOT treat as a clean init. Before writing any template:
    34	- Read `spec.md` §10.3 ("Adapting to Existing Projects") for the full procedure.
    35	- In short: scan existing files to reconstruct project history; propose (not impose) a draft WORKLOG reflecting past phases; ask the user to confirm/correct before writing; register existing files in FILE_INDEX in bulk per §4.4 if there are many (>~20 files); mark any superseded documents per §9.2.
    36	- The goal is to **describe reality faithfully**, not to pretend the project just started.
    37	
    38	**(d) Non-empty directory, user explicitly requests a clean start** (e.g., "ignore the existing files, I'm starting fresh on a new task"): this is the escape hatch from (c). Confirm explicitly with the user — "Existing files will NOT be reconstructed into WORKLOG; they remain on disk but are not represented in the documentation system. Do you want to proceed with clean init?" — and if the user confirms, proceed as (a). Record the user's override decision in WORKLOG's first phase summary so future agents understand why no prior history was reconstructed.
    39

    41

    43

    46

    48	**Current phase**: [PHASE_NAME] (⏳)
    49	**One-line status (as of [TODAY])**: [DESCRIPTION] — project just initialized
    50	
    51	---
    52	
    53	## Recovery Chain
    54	
    55	Recovery Chain is the entry ritual for any agent or human resuming work on this project.
    56	It has two layers.
    57	
    58	### Must-read (baseline)
    59	
    60	1. This file (CLAUDE.md)
    61	2. `CURRENT_STATUS.md`
    62	
    63	### Task-conditional
    64	
    65	- If looking up a specific file: read `FILE_INDEX.md`
    66	- If investigating historical phase details: read `WORKLOG.md`
    67	- [Add project-specific entries as work categories emerge]
    68	
    69	### Meta-rules
    70	
    71	- Recovery Chain is **self-contained**: every entry points to a file inside the project
    72	  (or a stable sibling-project path). No dependency on agent-side features (memory,
    73	  chat history, external services).
    74	- Recovery Chain is **living**: review and update at phase transitions.
    75

    89

    93	
    94	---
    95	
    96	## Doc Harness — Operational Rules
    97	
    98	[INSERT FULL CONTENT OF operational_rules.md HERE]
    99	```
   100

Preserve **both sentinels and the `<!-- doc-harness-ops-version: N.N -->` version tag** — these delimit the region that future re-embeds (after a skill upgrade) and `/doc-harness check` §1.10 can safely locate and replace. **Re-embed semantics**: a future `init` pass or manual re-embed replaces ONLY the bytes between `<!-- doc-harness-ops-start -->` and `<!-- doc-harness-ops-end -->`. Any custom iron rules, project-specific sections, or other content outside the delimited region is preserved untouched.

   186

   190	- **Mechanism**: This project maintains `inbox/` (received messages) and `outbox/` (sent messages). Messages are Markdown files with YAML frontmatter; filename `YYYY-MM-DD-from-<source>-<topic>.md`.
   191	- **Why this is mandatory (if adopted)**: Cross-project information exchanged only in chat is lost on session end. File-based messages survive session boundaries and are discoverable by any future agent through this project's Recovery Chain.
   192	- **Receiving**: Recovery Chain checks `inbox/` for `status: unread`. Read → update to `status: read`. After acting on the message → `status: actioned`. Never edit received messages beyond the status field; to respond, write a new message.
   193	- **Sending**: Write to this project's `outbox/` (permanent sender-side record) AND copy the same file into the recipient project's `inbox/`. Record the exchange in CURRENT_STATUS so it is traceable next session.
   194	- **Snapshots over pointers**: When communicating numbers/deliverables to another project, put the value in the message body rather than referencing internal files.

     1	# Doc Harness — Check
     2	
     3	Audit the project's documentation health and reflect on working principles.
     4	
     5	Two purposes: (1) catch file-level problems, (2) remind yourself of the rules you should be following.
     6	
     7	---
     8	
     9	## Part 1: File Health Audit
    10	
    11	### 1.1 Core files exist?
    12	
    13	Look for these 4 core files in the current directory (or nearest parent with CLAUDE.md):
    14	- `CLAUDE.md`, `CURRENT_STATUS.md`, `FILE_INDEX.md`, `WORKLOG.md`
    15	
    16	Missing → `❌ MISSING: [file]`
    17	None found → `❌ No Doc Harness found. Use /doc-harness init.` → stop.
    18	
    19	Also check: `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` — this is the reference specification.
    20	- Present → `✅ Spec present`
    21	- Missing → `⚠️ DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md not found — recommended but not required. Deploy from skill directory if available.`
    22	
    23	### 1.2 CURRENT_STATUS freshness
    24	
    25	Read the "Last updated" date from CURRENT_STATUS.md (only the first 5 lines, not full file).
    26	- Today → `✅ Fresh`
    27	- 1-3 days → `⚠️ [N] days old`
    28	- >3 days → `❌ Stale — update or execute pause protocol`
    29	
    30	### 1.3 CLAUDE.md one-line status
    31	
    32	Read the "one-line status (as of DATE)" from CLAUDE.md (only the first 5 lines).
    33	- Date matches CURRENT_STATUS → `✅ Current`
    34	- Older → `⚠️ Stale`
    35	
    36	### 1.4 FILE_INDEX completeness (root and sub-indexes)
    37	
    38	Compare FILE_INDEX entries against actual files on disk. The algorithm is recursive — a project may have sub-FILE_INDEX.md files below the root, and each must be checked against its own subtree. Use this approach:
    39	
    40	```bash
    41	# Locate all FILE_INDEX.md files in the project (root + sub-indexes)
    42	find . -type f -name 'FILE_INDEX.md' \
    43	  -not -path "./_archive*" -not -path "./.git/*" -not -path "./node_modules/*" -not -path "./dist/*" \
    44	  | sort > /tmp/dh_indexes.txt
    45	
    46	# For each index, check its own subtree — BUT prune at any sub-index boundary
    47	# so a file like data/experiments/foo.md belongs to data/experiments/FILE_INDEX.md's
    48	# scope, not to data/FILE_INDEX.md's scope.
    49	while IFS= read -r INDEX; do
    50	  DIR="$(dirname "$INDEX")"
    51	  echo "── checking $INDEX (scope: $DIR) ──"
    52	
    53	  # Build exclusion list: directories that contain OTHER FILE_INDEX.md files
    54	  # strictly below DIR. These belong to their own sub-index's scope.
    55	  EXCLUDES=()
    56	  while IFS= read -r OTHER_INDEX; do
    57	    OTHER_DIR="$(dirname "$OTHER_INDEX")"
    58	    if [ "$OTHER_DIR" != "$DIR" ] && [[ "$OTHER_DIR" == "$DIR"* ]]; then
    59	      EXCLUDES+=("-not" "-path" "$OTHER_DIR/*" "-not" "-path" "$OTHER_DIR")
    60	    fi
    61	  done < /tmp/dh_indexes.txt
    62	
    63	  # Files actually present in this index's scope (pruned at sub-index boundaries)
    64	  find "$DIR" -maxdepth 10 -type f \
    65	    "${EXCLUDES[@]}" \
    66	    \( -name '*.md' -o -name '*.py' -o -name '*.tex' -o -name '*.json' -o -name '*.csv' -o -name '*.txt' -o -name '*.pdf' -o -name '*.png' -o -name '*.bib' \) \
    67	    -not -path "*/_archive/*" -not -path "*/.git/*" -not -path "*/node_modules/*" -not -path "*/dist/*" \
    68	    -not -path "*/inbox/*" -not -path "*/outbox/*" \
    69	    | sed "s|^$DIR/||" | sort > /tmp/dh_disk.txt
    70	
    71	  # Entries mentioned inside this index
    72	  grep -oE '`[^`]+\.(md|py|tex|json|csv|txt|pdf|png|bib)`' "$INDEX" | tr -d '`' | sort > /tmp/dh_entries.txt
    73	
    74	  echo "Unregistered (files on disk but not in $INDEX):"
    75	  comm -23 /tmp/dh_disk.txt /tmp/dh_entries.txt
    76	  echo "Ghosts (entries in $INDEX but no such file):"
    77	  comm -13 /tmp/dh_disk.txt /tmp/dh_entries.txt
    78	done < /tmp/dh_indexes.txt
    79	```
    80	
    81	Note: if a sub-directory has its own sub-`FILE_INDEX.md`, the parent index registers the *sub-index file* in one line (per spec §4.3). The detailed files below belong to the sub-index's check, not the parent's.
    82	
    83	- All files registered at every level → `✅ Complete (N indexes checked)`
    84	- Unregistered files found → `❌ UNREGISTERED: [list with which index should register them]`
    85	- Ghost entries found → `❌ GHOST: [list with which index holds the ghost]`
    86	
    87	**Token efficiency**: Read `FILE_INDEX.md` files and `find` output only. Do NOT read leaf document content.
    88	
    89	### 1.5 WORKLOG TOC consistency
    90	
    91	Read WORKLOG.md. Compare TOC table rows with actual `##` headings (use Grep, not full file read).
    92	- Match → `✅ Consistent`
    93	- Mismatch → `⚠️ TOC has [N] entries, [M] sections found`
    94	
    95	### 1.6 WORKLOG length
    96	
    97	Count total lines of WORKLOG.md (use `wc -l` or equivalent; do not read the full file).
    98	- <1000 lines → `✅ [N] lines`
    99	- 1000–1500 → `⚠️ [N] lines — consider archival (§5.5)`
   100	- >1500 → `❌ [N] lines — archival overdue`
   101	
   102	### 1.7 Inbox status (if inter-project comms adopted)
   103	
   104	If `inbox/` exists at project root, do all four sub-checks. Use Grep on the YAML `status:` line and on file-age (don't read message bodies).
   105	
   106	**(a) Unread count** (scope: direct children of `inbox/` only — exclude `inbox/_archive/` and `inbox/_malformed/` so quarantined and archived messages don't double-count here):
   107	- No `inbox/` → skip the whole §1.7
   108	- All messages `read` or `actioned` → `✅ Inbox clean (N total, 0 unread)`
   109	- Any `unread` → `⚠️ Inbox has N unread message(s) — action needed`
   110	
   111	**(b) Archival trigger** (ties to spec §14.4 rule 3):
   112	Count messages with `status: actioned` whose file-mtime is older than 30 days.
   113	- ≥5 such messages → `⚠️ Archival due: N actioned message(s) older than 30 days — move to inbox/_archive/ this session`
   114	- <5 → no action (reported only at ✅ level)
   115	
   116	**(c) Malformed messages** (ties to §14.8):
   117	Count files in `inbox/_malformed/` if that directory exists.
   118	- 0 or no directory → ✅
   119	- ≥1 → `⚠️ Malformed messages quarantined: N in inbox/_malformed/ — review`
   120	
   121	**(d) Recent outbox send without CURRENT_STATUS entry**:
   122	For each file in `outbox/` whose mtime is within the last 3 days, verify CURRENT_STATUS car body mentions it by filename.
   123	- All recent sends recorded → ✅
   124	- Missing entries → `⚠️ Outbox sends not logged in CURRENT_STATUS: [list]`
   125	
   126	### 1.8 Car body length (language-independent)
   127	
   128	Count lines in CURRENT_STATUS between the **car body heading** and the next `##` heading. Match either `## Current Work` or `## 当前工作` (both variants produced by init templates). Use Grep/line counting, not full read.
   129	- <200 → `✅ [N] lines`
   130	- 200–250 → `⚠️ Approaching limit`
   131	- >250 → `❌ Over limit — consider phase transition`
   132	
   133	### 1.9 Mid-transition coherence (spec §6.3.1)
   134	
   135	Read three values and compare — this detects a phase transition interrupted between Steps 1 and 5.
   136	
   137	- **A**: CLAUDE.md "current phase" / "当前阶段" line (first 10 lines; match either language).
   138	- **B**: WORKLOG TOC's newest entry (first `| ` row after the TOC heading).
   139	- **C**: CURRENT_STATUS tire tracks' newest phase summary (first `###` heading under "Recent Completed" / "近期已完成").
   140	
   141	If A, B, C are mutually coherent per spec §6.3.1's table → `✅ Coherent`.
   142	Otherwise → `❌ Mid-transition state detected: A=[...] B=[...] C=[...]. Apply §6.3.1 repair.`
   143	
   144	### 1.10 Embedded operational-rules version
   145	
   146	Grep for the HTML comment `<!-- doc-harness-ops-version: N.N -->` anywhere in CLAUDE.md (case-insensitive, one line).
   147	- Found and matches the version of the installed skill (e.g. `1.4`) → `✅ Operational rules up to date (vN.N)`
   148	- Found but older than installed skill → `⚠️ Operational rules snapshot is vX.X; installed skill is vY.Y — re-embed from operational_rules.md to upgrade`
   149	- Missing entirely → `⚠️ No version marker found — this CLAUDE.md predates v1.4 or was hand-edited. Recommend re-embedding operational_rules.md.`
   150	
   151	The installed skill's version is the `**Version**` line at the top of the installed `spec.md`. **Resolve the install path in this order** (first hit wins):
   152	
   153	1. Project-level: `<project_root>/.claude/skills/doc-harness/spec.md`
   154	2. User-level, Claude Code default on Unix: `$HOME/.claude/skills/doc-harness/spec.md`
   155	3. User-level, XDG override: `${XDG_CONFIG_HOME:-$HOME/.config}/claude/skills/doc-harness/spec.md`
   156	4. User-level, Windows: `%USERPROFILE%\.claude\skills\doc-harness\spec.md` (bash: `"$USERPROFILE/.claude/skills/doc-harness/spec.md"` — forward slashes work on Windows bash)
   157	
   158	If no install path resolves, report `⚠️ Cannot locate installed skill — run check from a project where skill is deployed, or install at one of the paths above.` Do not treat "installed version not found" as passing.
   159	
   160	---
   161

   199	   2. [step title 2]
   200	   3. [step title 3]
   201	   ...
   202	   → Do all these steps serve the SAME phase goal?

   233	## Language-independence note
   234	
   235	All Part-1 anchors (`## Current Work`, `## Recent Completed`, `## Next Steps`, `## Current Working Principles`, `Iron Rules`, `Driving Manual`, etc.) match **either English or Chinese** headings produced by `init.md` templates — implementations should Grep for either variant. A mixed-language project (e.g., Chinese CLAUDE.md but English CURRENT_STATUS) still checks correctly as long as each document uses one consistent language internally.

   255	[1.8] Car body:        ✅ N lines / ⚠️/❌

   257	[1.10] Ops-rules ver.: ✅ vN.N / ⚠️ vX.X (installed: vY.Y) — re-embed
   258	
   259	── Part 2: Principle Reflection ──
   260

   262	📋 Driving Manual: [list with reflections]
   263	📝 Write It Down: [status]
   264	🔄 Phase coherence: [step titles + assessment]
   265	🗺️ Recovery Chain: [two-layer? self-contained? promotions/demotions?]
   266	
   267	── Actions Needed ──
   268	[specific fixes for ❌/⚠️ items]
   269	═══════════════════════════════════════
   270	```
   271

    43	
    44	## 第一章 首要原则与概述
    45	
    46	### 1.1 首要原则："落笔为安"（Write It Down or Lose It）
    47	
    48	Context中的一切信息都是临时的。无论多重要的分析结果、多精妙的设计思路，只要没有**写入文件**并**注册到FILE_INDEX**，就等于不存在。
    49	
    50	- **落笔**：重要信息必须写入文件。不写 = 丢失。
    51	- **为安**：写入的文件必须注册到FILE_INDEX。不注册 = 虽存在但不可发现 = 等同于丢失。
    52	
    53	这条原则优先于一切效率考量。宁可多写一个文件，不可让信息只存在于context中。
    54	
    55	### 1.2 什么是状态文档体系
    56	
    57	状态文档体系是一个由四个核心文档组成的信息管理系统，服务于一个**项目**。
    58	
    59	| 文档 | 角色 | 核心职责 | 更新频率 |
    60	|------|------|---------|---------|
    61	| **CLAUDE.md** | 门牌 | 项目入口、恢复起点、项目级铁律 | 阶段切换时 |
    62	| **CURRENT_STATUS.md** | 行驶中的汽车 | 当前阶段活跃信息、近期历史摘要、下一步、阶段级原则 | 每个session |
    63	| **FILE_INDEX.md** | 图书馆目录 | 按类别索引项目所有文件 | 文件变化时 |
    64	| **WORKLOG.md** | 行车记录仪 | 永久保存所有阶段的完整工作详情 | 阶段切换时（批量） |
    65	
    66	### 1.3 核心场景
    67	
    68	| 场景 | 需求 |
    69	|------|------|
    70	| **全新Agent到达** | 读CLAUDE.md → CURRENT_STATUS → 知道做什么 |
    71	| **Context compact后恢复** | 读CURRENT_STATUS → 从车身恢复到中断点 |
    72	| **跨项目切换** | 读目标项目CLAUDE.md → 快速了解 |
    73	| **工作过程中** | 实时更新CURRENT_STATUS车身 + 新文件注册FILE_INDEX |
    74	
    75	### 1.4 不依赖外部记忆系统
    76	
    77	状态文档体系完全自足。不依赖MEMORY.md、不依赖对话历史、不依赖任何Agent的私有记忆。任何Agent仅凭阅读文件即可完全恢复工作状态。
    78	
    79	如果环境提供了记忆系统（如Claude Code的MEMORY.md），可以作为**补充加速**（提供额外上下文），但不作为恢复的必要条件。
    80	
    81	---
    82	
    83	## 第二章 CLAUDE.md — 入口文档
    84	
    85	### 2.1 职责
    86	- 告诉来者"这是什么项目"
    87	- 提供恢复链（阅读顺序）
    88	- 定义项目级铁律（永久有效，不随阶段变化）
    89	- 指向其他三个核心文档
    90	- 提供项目特有的稳定技术信息
    91	
    92	### 2.2 不做什么
    93	- 不记录详细当前状态（→ CURRENT_STATUS）
    94	- 不罗列所有文件（→ FILE_INDEX）
    95	- 不记录历史工作详情（→ WORKLOG）
    96	
    97	### 2.3 模板
    98	
    99	CLAUDE.md由三部分组成：项目特定信息 + 操作版规则（嵌入） + 完整版规范指针。
   100

我现在已经完成了充分的调研。让我总结关键发现：

## 当前状态分析

### WhoAMI 报告的核心问题
1. **Agent 身份混乱事件 (INC-2026-04-22-001)**：WhoAMI agent 在调研 lit-system-api 代码时，把自己当成了 lit 项目的代理，导致越界写入、修改对方文档、发信 from 字段写错。
2. **根本原因**：
   - 直接原因：项目身份认知错误
   - 触发因素：跨项目深度调研导致认知漂移
   - 深层原因：Recovery Chain 缺乏身份校验
   - 机制缺陷：doc-harness 未规范身份锚定

### 当前 doc-harness 规范的缺口

**缺口 A (P0)**：CLAUDE.md 模板**没有**要求 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
- 当前 CLAUDE.md 模板（§2.3）的结构：项目信息 → Recovery Chain → Project Overview → Iron Rules → Key Technical → Sub-projects → Operational Rules
- **没有**在最顶部放置身份锁定的要求
- WhoAMI 已在自己的 CLAUDE.md 顶部添加了 `🔒 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK`，这是一个成功的参考实现

**缺口 B (P0)**：跨项目操作 checklist
- INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC.md 有 iron rule 模板，但**没有**一个标准化的 cross-project operation checklist
- WhoAMI 报告提出的 checklist 项：确认 from 字段、确认 outbox 路径、确认 inbox 路径、确认未修改对方内部文档

**缺口 C (P1)**：Recovery Chain 规范增加 Step 0「身份校验」
- 当前 §11.1 Session Start 流程：Read must-read → Scan task-conditional → Confirm with user / Continue per headlights
- **没有**显式的身份确认步骤

**缺口 D (P1)**：/doc-harness check 增加身份锁验证
- 当前 check.md §2.5 Recovery Chain health 检查：是否两层结构、must-read ≤ 3、是否 self-contained、晋升/降级
- **没有**检查 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 是否存在

## 设计解决方案

### 核心设计决策

**问题：AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 应该放在哪里？**

选项：
1. 放在 CLAUDE.md 最顶部（WhoAMI 方案）
2. 放在 Recovery Chain 的 must-read 层里（作为 Step 0）
3. 放在 Iron Rules 里（作为一个 iron rule）
4. 放在一个新的独立区块

分析：
- WhoAMI 放在最顶部的方案已经经过实战验证（4/22 事件后立即实施，用户确认有效）
- 放在最顶部的好处：agent 读 CLAUDE.md 的第一眼就看到，防止后续阅读中认知漂移
- 放在 Recovery Chain 里的问题：Recovery Chain 是一个"读什么"的指令，不是一个"你是谁"的声明
- 放在 Iron Rules 里的问题：Iron Rules 是"做什么/不做什么"的规则，但 identity 是一个"你是谁"的认知锚定
- **最佳位置**：CLAUDE.md 最顶部、标题下方、所有其他内容之前。这是一个**认知锚定**，不是规则。

**问题：AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 的内容应该是什么？**

参考 WhoAMI 的实现，结合通用化需求：
- 声明"你是 X 项目的代理"
- 声明"你的职责是..."
- 声明"你永远不是 Y 项目的代理"
- 列出"绝对禁止"（越界行为）
- 列出"唯一允许的跨项目交互"
- 声明"违反后果"
- 自检提示

但 doc-harness 是一个 skill/框架，不能硬编码具体项目名。需要在模板中使用占位符，由 init 填充。

**问题：是否所有项目都需要 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK？**

- 如果项目是 standalone（无跨项目通信），identity lock 仍然有价值——防止 agent 在调研外部资源时产生认知漂移
- 但 standalone 项目的 identity lock 可以更简单（只需要声明"你是 X 的代理"）
- 采用跨项目通信的项目需要完整版（包含跨项目交互规则）
- **方案**：所有项目都有基础版 identity lock，启用 inbox/outbox 的项目有扩展版

**问题：跨项目操作 checklist 应该放在哪里？**

- 这不是一个"文档"或"规则"，而是一个**操作流程**
- 最合适的位置：operational_rules.md 的 Inter-Project Communication 部分，作为发送流程的子步骤
- 或者：在 spec §14.3.1 Pre-send verification 之后，添加一个 Pre-send checklist

**问题：Recovery Chain 的 Step 0 怎么设计？**

- 当前 §11.1 的 session start 流程已经是结构化的
- 可以在 Read must-read 之前加一个**心理锚定步骤**：
  "在读取任何项目文件之前，确认你的身份：你是 [PROJECT_NAME] 的代理。"
- 但这不应该是一个必须"读"的文件步骤，而是一个**认知仪式**
- 方案：在 operational_rules.md 的 Recovery Chain 部分增加一个前置说明

**问题：check 怎么验证 identity lock？**

- check.md §2.5 Recovery Chain health 已经很接近
- 增加一项：检查 CLAUDE.md 最顶部（前 30 行）是否包含身份声明
- 检查内容包括：项目名称声明、职责声明、跨项目边界声明（如果启用了 inbox/outbox）

### 完整方案

让我设计一个全面的升级方案，涉及以下文件：

1. **spec.md** — 修改 §2.3 CLAUDE.md 模板，在最顶部添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
2. **spec.md** — 修改 §11.1 Session Start，添加身份确认仪式
3. **spec.md** — 修改 §14.3 / §14.3.1，添加跨项目操作 checklist
4. **spec.md** — 版本历史更新到 v1.5.2 或 v1.6.0
5. **operational_rules.md** — 修改 Recovery Chain 部分，添加身份锚定
6. **operational_rules.md** — 修改 Inter-Project Communication 部分，添加发送 checklist
7. **init.md** — 修改 CLAUDE.md 模板，添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
8. **check.md** — 修改 §2.5，添加 identity lock 验证

10. **CLAUDE.md (项目根)** — 添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
11. **kimi-skill/references/** — 同步更新

等等，让我重新思考版本号。这个改动很大（新增 identity lock 作为核心要求），应该是一个 minor 版本升级。从 v1.5.1 → v1.6.0？还是 v1.5.2？

看版本历史：
- v1.5.0: sync + flush commands
- v1.5.1: recall command (这是当前版本)

这个改动涉及：
- CLAUDE.md 模板结构变化（新增 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK）
- Recovery Chain 行为变化（Step 0 身份确认）
- Inter-project 流程变化（发送 checklist）
- check 流程变化（identity lock 验证）

这是一个**重大的规范升级**，影响所有新项目初始化 + 所有现有项目的 CLAUDE.md 结构。应该是 v1.6.0。

所以我现在只需要做调查研究 + 撰写计划文件，不需要实际执行修改。

### 方案选择

经过充分分析，我认为最佳方案是：

**方案：AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 作为 CLAUDE.md 强制前置结构**

**理由**：
1. WhoAMI 的实战验证表明，放在最顶部的 identity lock 能有效防止认知漂移
2. 跨项目通信已经是 doc-harness 的成熟功能（Chapter 14），身份混乱是其最大风险
3. 所有项目都有"我是谁"的问题，即使 standalone 项目也可能在调研外部资源时产生混淆
4. 将 identity lock 嵌入 CLAUDE.md 模板，确保每个新项目天生具备防护

**具体设计**：

1. **CLAUDE.md 模板结构更新**：
   ```
   # [PROJECT_NAME] — Entry Document
   
   > 🔒 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
   > 
   > 你是 [PROJECT_NAME] 项目的代理。
   > [如果启用了 inbox/outbox:]
   > 你不是任何其他项目的代理。
   
   ---
   
   **Last updated**: ...
   ```

2. **operational_rules.md Recovery Chain 更新**：
   - 在"Applying at session start"步骤中，Step 0: "确认身份：阅读 CLAUDE.md 的 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 段落，确认你是该项目的代理。"

3. **spec §14 发送 checklist**：
   - 在 §14.3.1 Pre-send verification 之后，添加 §14.3.2 Pre-send checklist：
     - [ ] from 字段写的是本项目的名称
     - [ ] 文件写入的是本项目的 outbox/
     - [ ] 复制到的是接收方的 inbox/（不是 outbox/）
     - [ ] 没有修改接收方的内部文档

4. **check.md §2.5 更新**：
   - 增加 identity lock 检查：CLAUDE.md 前 30 行是否包含 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK

5. **版本号**：v1.6.0（重大规范升级）

**双语同步**：所有 skill/ 修改必须同步到 skill-zh/。

**向后兼容性**：
- 现有项目的 CLAUDE.md 不需要立即修改（identity lock 是推荐性补充，不是破坏性变更）
- 但 check 会报告缺少 identity lock 的警告
- init 创建的新项目将自带 identity lock

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

我已经完成了充分的调研。现在需要撰写计划文件，然后调用 ExitPlanMode。

让我整理调研结果和设计一个全面的方案：

## 核心发现

### 缺口分析

1. **缺口 A (P0)**：doc-harness 规范**未要求** CLAUDE.md 包含 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
   - 当前 §2.3 模板结构：标题 → Last updated/phase/status → Recovery Chain → Overview → Iron Rules → ...
   - WhoAMI 在事件后在 CLAUDE.md 最顶部添加了 `🔒 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK`，经用户验证有效
   - 这是防止认知漂移的最前线防御

2. **缺口 B (P0)**：跨项目操作**没有标准化 checklist**
   - §14.3.1 有 pre-send verification（确认接收方已采纳协议）
   - 但**没有**防止发信方自己犯错的 checklist（from 字段、outbox 路径、不修改对方文档）
   - WhoAMI 事件中的 4 个错误（向 lit outbox 写入、修改 lit FILE_INDEX、修改 lit CURRENT_STATUS、from 字段写 lit）都没有被现有流程阻止

3. **缺口 C (P1)**：Recovery Chain 的 session start 流程**没有身份确认步骤**
   - 当前 §11.1：Read must-read → Scan task-conditional → Confirm with user / Continue
   - 缺少一个"在读取项目文件之前，先确认自己是谁"的心理锚定

4. **缺口 D (P1)**：check 流程**没有验证 identity lock**
   - §2.5 Recovery Chain health 检查结构、self-contained、晋升/降级
   - 缺少"是否存在 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK"的检查

## 方案设计

### 关键设计决策

**Q1: Identity lock 放在哪里？**

候选位置：
- a) CLAUDE.md 最顶部（标题下方，所有内容之前）— WhoAMI 方案
- b) Recovery Chain must-read 的第一步（作为一个必须"读"的条目）
- c) Iron Rules 的一部分（作为一个规则）
- d) 独立的 IDENTITY.md 文件

分析：
- a) **最推荐**。身份锚定不是"一个要读的文件"，而是"在开始读任何内容之前，先确认自己是谁"。放在最顶部确保 agent 在读取任何项目信息之前先建立身份认知。WhoAMI 实战已验证。
- b) 不合适。Recovery Chain 是"读什么"的指令列表，identity lock 不是另一个要读的文件。
- c) 不合适。Iron Rules 是行为规范（"不要做什么"），identity lock 是认知锚定（"你是谁"）。
- d) 过度设计。多一个文件增加认知负担，且 Recovery Chain 需要指向它，增加 must-read 层大小。

**Q2: Identity lock 的内容模板？**

需要包含：
- 项目名称声明（你是 X 的代理）
- 职责简述（你做什么）
- 跨项目边界声明（你不是其他项目的代理）
- 绝对禁止行为列表（越界操作）
- 唯一允许的跨项目交互方式
- 违反后果
- 自检提示

但 doc-harness 是通用框架，不能硬编码具体项目信息。需要在 init 时用占位符填充。

**Q3: 是否所有项目都需要？**

- Standalone 项目：也需要基础 identity lock（防止在调研外部库/文档时产生认知漂移）
- 启用 inbox/outbox 的项目：需要完整版（包含跨项目交互边界）
- **方案**：所有项目都有基础版，启用跨项目通信的有扩展版

**Q4: Checklist 放在哪里？**

- Pre-send checklist 属于操作流程，不是文档规范
- 最佳位置：spec §14 的跨项目通信章节，作为发送流程的标准步骤
- 在 operational_rules.md 的 inbox/outbox 部分也嵌入简化版

**Q5: 版本号？**

- v1.5.1 → v1.6.0（重大规范升级：新增强制结构 + 新流程 + check 新项）
- 或 v1.5.2（如果是小修补）
- 判断：新增 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK 作为 CLAUDE.md 的强制前置结构，改变了核心文档的模板。这是架构级变更。→ v1.6.0

### 实施文件清单

| 文件 | 变更 |
|------|------|
| `skill/spec.md` | §2.3 模板添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK；§11.1 添加 Step 0 身份确认；§14 添加发送 checklist；版本历史更新 |
| `skill/operational_rules.md` | Recovery Chain 添加身份锚定说明；inbox/outbox 部分添加发送 checklist |
| `skill/init.md` | CLAUDE.md 模板添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK（占位符）；Step 3.6 扩展为启用 inbox/outbox 时的扩展版 |
| `skill/check.md` | §2.5 添加 identity lock 验证；§1.x 新增 identity lock 文件健康检查 |
| `skill-zh/spec.md` | 同步所有变更 |
| `skill-zh/operational_rules.md` | 同步所有变更 |
| `skill-zh/init.md` | 同步所有变更 |
| `skill-zh/check.md` | 同步所有变更 |
| `kimi-skill/references/` | 同步更新的引用文件 |
| `CLAUDE.md` (项目根) | 添加 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK |
| `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` (项目根) | 更新（从 skill/spec.md 同步）|

### 双语同步（铁律 1）

所有 skill/ 变更必须镜像到 skill-zh/。

### 风险评估

| 风险 | 等级 | 缓解 |
|------|------|------|
| 现有项目 CLAUDE.md 模板变更导致格式不兼容 | 低 | Identity lock 是纯新增内容，不影响现有结构解析 |
| Identity lock 成为形式主义（agent 忽略） | 中 | 在 operational_rules 中明确要求"在读取任何文件之前先确认身份"；check 验证其存在 |
| 模板过于冗长 | 低 | 控制在 15-20 行；standalone 项目用精简版 |
| 版本升级后 operational_rules 嵌入区需要重新嵌入 | 中 | 正常升级流程，check §1.10 会检测并提示 |

现在撰写计划文件。

```json
{
  "path": "C:\\Users\\ZY\\.kimi\\plans\\nightwing-valkyrie-aquaman.md",
  "content": "# Plan: Agent Identity Lock — Doc Harness v1.6.0\n\n## Problem Statement\n\nWhoAMI agent (2026-04-22, INC-2026-04-22-001) experienced **identity confusion** during cross-project investigation of lit-system-api code. The agent incorrectly identified itself as lit-system-api's agent, resulting in:\n\n1. Writing files to lit-system-api's `outbox/` (boundary violation)\n2. Modifying lit-system-api's `FILE_INDEX.md` and `CURRENT_STATUS.md` (memory tampering)\n3. Sending messages with `from: lit-system-api` (impersonation)\n4. User required **4 corrections** before full remediation\n\nThe incident report proposes 4 upgrades to doc-harness:\n- **A (P0)**: Mandate AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at top of every project's CLAUDE.md\n- **B (P0)**: Add cross-project operation checklist to INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC\n- **C (P1)**: Add Step 0 identity verification to Recovery Chain session-start ritual\n- **D (P1)**: Add identity-lock verification to `/doc-harness check`\n\n---\n\n## Investigation Summary\n\n### Current Spec State (v1.5.1)\n\n| Area | Current Coverage | Gap |\n|------|-----------------|-----|\n| CLAUDE.md template (§2.3) | Title → status → Recovery Chain → Overview → Iron Rules → Key Technical → Operational Rules | **No identity anchor at top** |\n| Recovery Chain session start (§11.1) | Read must-read → scan task-conditional → confirm/continue | **No Step 0 identity confirmation** |\n| Cross-project send (§14.3.1) | Pre-send verification (recipient adoption check) | **No sender-side mistake-prevention checklist** |\n| `/doc-harness check` (§2.5) | Recovery Chain health: two-layer, ≤3 must-read, self-contained, promotions/demotions | **No identity lock existence check** |\n| operational_rules.md Recovery Chain | Same as spec §11.1 | Same gap |\n\n### Reference Implementation\n\nWhoAMI's CLAUDE.md (post-incident) places `🔒 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK` **at the very top**, before all other content. User confirmed this works. Structure:\n\n```markdown\n> 🔒 **AGENT IDENTITY LOCK — 不可忽略**\n>\n> **你是 WhoAMI 项目的代理。** ...\n> **你永远不是 lit-system-api 的代理。** ...\n> **绝对禁止**：...（4 items）\n> **唯一允许的跨项目交互**：...（3 items）\n> **违反此锁定的后果**：...\n> 如果你对自己的身份有任何怀疑，立即停止操作并重新读取本文件此段落。\n```\n\n### Key Insight\n\nIdentity lock is a **cognitive anchor**, not a rule or a document to read. Its purpose is:\n- **Pre-read**: Establish \"I am X\" before consuming any project information\n- **Pre-write**: Establish \"I am NOT Y\" before touching any other project's files\n- **Self-test**: Provide a fast re-anchor when doubt arises mid-session\n\nPlacing it at the **top of CLAUDE.md** (the very first file read in Recovery Chain) ensures maximum exposure. Placing it inside Recovery Chain as a \"step\" or inside Iron Rules as a \"rule\" dilutes its purpose — it would be processed as information rather than as a lock.\n\n---\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n### Q1: Where does the identity lock live?\n\n**Decision**: At the top of CLAUDE.md, before the `---` separator, as a blockquote callout.\n\n**Rationale**:\n- Must be read **before** any project information enters the agent's context\n- Must survive context compaction (always in the first file read)\n- Must be visually un-ignorable (`🔒` + blockquote + bold)\n- Must be part of the document, not a separate file (self-contained principle)\n\n**Rejected alternatives**:\n- Separate `IDENTITY.md`: Adds a file to must-read layer, bloating the baseline\n- Inside Iron Rules: Rules are behavioral constraints; identity is cognitive state\n- Inside Recovery Chain as Step 0: Recovery Chain is a reading order; identity lock is a pre-reading mental ritual\n\n### Q2: What goes in the identity lock?\n\n**Decision**: Two-tier template — **Base** (all projects) + **Extended** (inbox/outbox enabled).\n\n**Base** (all projects, ~8 lines):\n```markdown\n> 🔒 **AGENT IDENTITY LOCK**\n>\n> **你是 [PROJECT_NAME] 项目的代理。**\n> 你的职责：[1-sentence from init context].\n>\n> 如果你对自己的身份有任何怀疑，立即停止操作并重新读取本段落。\n```\n\n**Extended** (inbox/outbox projects, adds ~12 lines):\n```markdown\n> **你不是任何其他项目的代理。** 其他项目由各自的 agent 维护。\n>\n> **绝对禁止**：\n> - 修改其他项目的代码、配置文件或内部文档\n> - 向其他项目的 outbox/ 写入文件\n> - 以其他项目的名义发信（from 字段写错项目名）\n>\n> **唯一允许的跨项目交互**：\n> - 发信：写入本项目的 outbox/（from: [PROJECT_NAME]）+ 复制到对方 inbox/\n> - 部署：仅部署对方提供的 commit/tag（不可自行修改）\n> - 读取：只读对方 inbox/ 中的回复（只读）\n```\n\n**Rationale**: Standalone projects still face identity risk (investigating external libraries, copying code from other repos). The base lock is universal. The extended lock adds cross-project boundaries only when needed.\n\n### Q3: How does Recovery Chain incorporate identity verification?\n\n**Decision**: Add a **pre-step** to the session-start ritual in operational_rules.md:\n\n```\nApplying Recovery Chain at session start:\n0. Identity anchor: Read the AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at the top of CLAUDE.md.\n   Confirm: \"I am [PROJECT_NAME]'s agent. I am NOT any other project's agent.\"\n1. Read must-read layer in order...\n```\n\n**Rationale**: Step 0 is a **cognitive act**, not a file-read act. It frames all subsequent reading. Without it, an agent reading deeply into another project's code (e.g., during dependency investigation) may absorb that project's context and drift.\n\n### Q4: Where does the cross-project send checklist go?\n\n**Decision**: Insert as **§14.3.2 Pre-send Checklist** in spec, and mirror in operational_rules.md inbox/outbox section.\n\nChecklist (5 items):\n```markdown\nBefore writing a cross-project message, verify:\n- [ ] `from:` field contains THIS project's name (not recipient's)\n- [ ] Message is written to THIS project's `outbox/` (not recipient's)\n- [ ] Copy targets recipient's `inbox/` (not their `outbox/`)\n- [ ] I have NOT modified any of recipient's internal documents\n- [ ] Recipient's inbox/outbox protocol is active (§14.3.1 verification passed)\n```\n\n**Rationale**: §14.3.1 already has recipient-side verification. The checklist is sender-side self-defense. ## Approved Plan:
# Plan: Agent Identity Lock — Doc Harness v1.6.0

## Problem Statement

WhoAMI agent (2026-04-22, INC-2026-04-22-001) experienced **identity confusion** during cross-project investigation of lit-system-api code. The agent incorrectly identified itself as lit-system-api's agent, resulting in:

1. Writing files to lit-system-api's `outbox/` (boundary violation)
2. Modifying lit-system-api's `FILE_INDEX.md` and `CURRENT_STATUS.md` (memory tampering)
3. Sending messages with `from: lit-system-api` (impersonation)
4. User required **4 corrections** before full remediation

The incident report proposes 4 upgrades to doc-harness:
- **A (P0)**: Mandate AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at top of every project's CLAUDE.md
- **B (P0)**: Add cross-project operation checklist to INTERPROJECT_COMM_SPEC
- **C (P1)**: Add Step 0 identity verification to Recovery Chain session-start ritual
- **D (P1)**: Add identity-lock verification to `/doc-harness check`

---

## Investigation Summary

### Current Spec State (v1.5.1)

| Area | Current Coverage | Gap |
|------|-----------------|-----|
| CLAUDE.md template (§2.3) | Title → status → Recovery Chain → Overview → Iron Rules → Key Technical → Operational Rules | **No identity anchor at top** |
| Recovery Chain session start (§11.1) | Read must-read → scan task-conditional → confirm/continue | **No Step 0 identity confirmation** |
| Cross-project send (§14.3.1) | Pre-send verification (recipient adoption check) | **No sender-side mistake-prevention checklist** |
| `/doc-harness check` (§2.5) | Recovery Chain health: two-layer, ≤3 must-read, self-contained, promotions/demotions | **No identity lock existence check** |
| operational_rules.md Recovery Chain | Same as spec §11.1 | Same gap |

### Reference Implementation

WhoAMI's CLAUDE.md (post-incident) places `🔒 AGENT IDENTITY LOCK` **at the very top**, before all other content. User confirmed this works. Structure:

```markdown
> 🔒 **AGENT IDENTITY LOCK — 不可忽略**
>
> **你是 WhoAMI 项目的代理。** ...
> **你永远不是 lit-system-api 的代理。** ...
> **绝对禁止**：...（4 items）
> **唯一允许的跨项目交互**：...（3 items）
> **违反此锁定的后果**：...
> 如果你对自己的身份有任何怀疑，立即停止操作并重新读取本文件此段落。
```

### Key Insight

Identity lock is a **cognitive anchor**, not a rule or a document to read. Its purpose is:
- **Pre-read**: Establish "I am X" before consuming any project information
- **Pre-write**: Establish "I am NOT Y" before touching any other project's files
- **Self-test**: Provide a fast re-anchor when doubt arises mid-session

Placing it at the **top of CLAUDE.md** (the very first file read in Recovery Chain) ensures maximum exposure. Placing it inside Recovery Chain as a "step" or inside Iron Rules as a "rule" dilutes its purpose — it would be processed as information rather than as a lock.

---

## Design Decisions

### Q1: Where does the identity lock live?

**Decision**: At the top of CLAUDE.md, before the `---` separator, as a blockquote callout.

**Rationale**:
- Must be read **before** any project information enters the agent's context
- Must survive context compaction (always in the first file read)
- Must be visually un-ignorable (`🔒` + blockquote + bold)
- Must be part of the document, not a separate file (self-contained principle)

**Rejected alternatives**:
- Separate `IDENTITY.md`: Adds a file to must-read layer, bloating the baseline
- Inside Iron Rules: Rules are behavioral constraints; identity is cognitive state
- Inside Recovery Chain as Step 0: Recovery Chain is a reading order; identity lock is a pre-reading mental ritual

### Q2: What goes in the identity lock?

**Decision**: Two-tier template — **Base** (all projects) + **Extended** (inbox/outbox enabled).

**Base** (all projects, ~8 lines):
```markdown
> 🔒 **AGENT IDENTITY LOCK**
>
> **你是 [PROJECT_NAME] 项目的代理。**
> 你的职责：[1-sentence from init context].
>
> 如果你对自己的身份有任何怀疑，立即停止操作并重新读取本段落。
```

**Extended** (inbox/outbox projects, adds ~12 lines):
```markdown
> **你不是任何其他项目的代理。** 其他项目由各自的 agent 维护。
>
> **绝对禁止**：
> - 修改其他项目的代码、配置文件或内部文档
> - 向其他项目的 outbox/ 写入文件
> - 以其他项目的名义发信（from 字段写错项目名）
>
> **唯一允许的跨项目交互**：
> - 发信：写入本项目的 outbox/（from: [PROJECT_NAME]）+ 复制到对方 inbox/
> - 部署：仅部署对方提供的 commit/tag（不可自行修改）
> - 读取：只读对方 inbox/ 中的回复（只读）
```

**Rationale**: Standalone projects still face identity risk (investigating external libraries, copying code from other repos). The base lock is universal. The extended lock adds cross-project boundaries only when needed.

### Q3: How does Recovery Chain incorporate identity verification?

**Decision**: Add a **pre-step** to the session-start ritual in operational_rules.md:

```
Applying Recovery Chain at session start:
0. Identity anchor: Read the AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at the top of CLAUDE.md.
   Confirm: "I am [PROJECT_NAME]'s agent. I am NOT any other project's agent."
1. Read must-read layer in order...
```

**Rationale**: Step 0 is a **cognitive act**, not a file-read act. It frames all subsequent reading. Without it, an agent reading deeply into another project's code (e.g., during dependency investigation) may absorb that project's context and drift.

### Q4: Where does the cross-project send checklist go?

**Decision**: Insert as **§14.3.2 Pre-send Checklist** in spec, and mirror in operational_rules.md inbox/outbox section.

Checklist (5 items):
```markdown
Before writing a cross-project message, verify:
- [ ] `from:` field contains THIS project's name (not recipient's)
- [ ] Message is written to THIS project's `outbox/` (not recipient's)
- [ ] Copy targets recipient's `inbox/` (not their `outbox/`)
- [ ] I have NOT modified any of recipient's internal documents
- [ ] Recipient's inbox/outbox protocol is active (§14.3.1 verification passed)
```

**Rationale**: §14.3.1 already has recipient-side verification. The checklist is sender-side self-defense. It directly addresses all 4 errors in INC-2026-04-22-001.

### Q5: How does check verify the identity lock?

**Decision**: Two new check items:

**Part 1 (file health)**: New §1.11 — Identity Lock Presence
- Read first 30 lines of CLAUDE.md
- Check for: `AGENT IDENTITY LOCK` string + project name declaration + self-test prompt
- Result: `✅ Present` / `⚠️ Missing or incomplete`

**Part 2 (principle reflection)**: Extend §2.5 Recovery Chain health
- Add: `→ Does CLAUDE.md begin with an AGENT IDENTITY LOCK?`

### Q6: Version number?

**Decision**: v1.6.0

**Rationale**: This is an **architectural change** to the core document template (CLAUDE.md gains a mandatory new top-level structural element) plus new behavioral rituals (Step 0 identity anchor) plus new check items. Per semantic-ish versioning: new feature area (identity security) = minor bump. Patch would understate the impact.

---

## Recommended Implementation Plan

### Phase 1: Update Core Spec (skill/spec.md + skill-zh/spec.md)

| Section | Change |
|---------|--------|
| §2.3 CLAUDE.md Template | Add AGENT IDENTITY LOCK blockquote at top, before `---` separator. Include base+extended variants with `[PROJECT_NAME]` placeholder. |
| §11.1 Session Start | Insert Step 0: "Identity anchor — read AGENT IDENTITY LOCK and confirm project identity." |
| §14.3.2 (new) | Add Pre-send Checklist with 5 verification items. |
| §14.5 Integration | Add note: "CLAUDE.md iron rules block should reference AGENT IDENTITY LOCK." |
| Appendix B (Quick Checklist) | Add: "Identity lock present in CLAUDE.md?" |
| Version History | Add v1.6.0 entry. |

### Phase 2: Update Operational Rules (skill/operational_rules.md + skill-zh/)

| Section | Change |
|---------|--------|
| Recovery Chain (Session Start) | Add Step 0 identity anchor ritual. |
| Optional Inter-Project Communication | Add Pre-send Checklist after receiving/sending descriptions. |
| Version tag | Bump to `1.6.0`. |

### Phase 3: Update Init (skill/init.md + skill-zh/)

| Section | Change |
|---------|--------|
| File 1: CLAUDE.md | Add AGENT IDENTITY LOCK placeholder block at top. Base version always. Extended version appended when inbox/outbox enabled. |
| Step 3.6 | Extended identity lock auto-included when inter-project comms enabled. |
| Step 4: Verify | Add: "AGENT IDENTITY LOCK present at top of CLAUDE.md?" |

### Phase 4: Update Check (skill/check.md + skill-zh/)

| Section | Change |
|---------|--------|
| §1.11 (new) | Identity Lock Presence check (first 30 lines of CLAUDE.md). |
| §2.5 Recovery Chain health | Add identity lock verification item. |
| Output Format | Add `[1.11] Identity lock: ✅/⚠️` line. |

### Phase 5: Update Project Root Files

| File | Change |
|------|--------|
| `CLAUDE.md` (project root) | Add AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at top. |
| `DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md` (project root) | Re-sync from skill/spec.md after Phase 1. |
| `skill/SKILL.md` + `skill-zh/SKILL.md` | Update version references, argument-hint if needed. |
| `kimi-skill/` | Sync reference files. |

### Phase 6: Deploy

1. Bump version numbers across all files (spec.md, operational_rules.md, READMEs, etc.)
2. Bilingual sync verification (skill-zh/ mirrors skill/)
3. Git commit + push to both repos
4. Update installed copies (`~/.claude/skills/doc-harness/`, `~/.kimi/skills/doc-harness/`)
5. Mark inbox messages status: actioned (with note referencing v1.6.0)

---

## Impact Assessment

### Affected Files (14 files)

```
skill/spec.md                    ← §2.3, §11.1, §14, Appendix B, version history
skill/operational_rules.md       ← Recovery Chain, inbox/outbox section, version tag
skill/init.md                    ← CLAUDE.md template, Step 3.6, Step 4
skill/check.md                   ← §1.11, §2.5, output format
skill/SKILL.md                   ← version reference
skill-zh/spec.md                 ← bilingual mirror
skill-zh/operational_rules.md    ← bilingual mirror
skill-zh/init.md                 ← bilingual mirror
skill-zh/check.md                ← bilingual mirror
skill-zh/SKILL.md                ← bilingual mirror
CLAUDE.md                        ← add AGENT IDENTITY LOCK
DOC_HARNESS_SPEC.md              ← re-sync from spec.md
README.md                        ← version badge
README_zh.md                     ← version badge
```

### Backward Compatibility

- **Existing projects**: Not broken. Identity lock is a new structural element, not a change to existing elements. Old CLAUDE.md files remain valid. `/doc-harness check` will report `⚠️ Identity lock missing` as a recommendation, not a failure.
- **New projects**: Will receive identity lock at init time.
- **Operational rules re-embed**: Check §1.10 will detect the version bump (`1.5.1 → 1.6.0`) and prompt re-embedding. This is normal upgrade behavior.

### Risk Analysis

| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|------|-----------|--------|------------|
| Identity lock ignored by agents (formalism) | Medium | High | Blockquote + 🔒 + bold + "不可忽略" make it visually salient. Step 0 ritual in operational rules makes it procedurally mandatory. Check verifies existence. |
| Template too verbose | Low | Low | Base version is 8 lines. Extended adds 12 only for inbox/outbox projects. |
| Bilingual sync drift | Low | High | Iron Rule 1 enforcement. Phase-by-phase sync checklist. |
| Version history table in spec.md becomes unwieldy | Low | Low | v1.6.0 entry is one row. |

---

## Alternative Approaches Considered (and Rejected)

### Alternative 1: Minimal Patch — Only add check item
- **Idea**: Don't change CLAUDE.md template. Just add a check warning when identity lock is missing.
- **Rejected**: Passive. Doesn't prevent future incidents. The root cause is cognitive, not procedural.

### Alternative 2: Separate `IDENTITY.md` file
- **Idea**: Create a new core document (5th document) for identity.
- **Rejected**: Violates self-contained minimalism. Adds a file to must-read layer. Recovery Chain would grow to 3 must-read items, weakening the two-layer design. Identity must be in the first file read, not a secondary file.

### Alternative 3: Identity lock inside Iron Rules
- **Idea**: Add "Know your project identity" as an iron rule.
- **Rejected**: Iron rules are behavioral ("don't do X"). Identity is cognitive ("you are Y"). A rule saying "don't confuse yourself with other projects" is unenforceable. A lock saying "you are X" is a cognitive anchor.

### Alternative 4: Version v1.5.2 instead of v1.6.0
- **Idea**: Treat this as a patch (bugfix) to the existing template.
- **Rejected**: Adding a mandatory new structural element to CLAUDE.md is not a bugfix. It changes how every new project is initialized. Minor version bump is more honest about impact.

---

## Recommendation

**Single recommendation**: Implement as described above (v1.6.0, AGENT IDENTITY LOCK at top of CLAUDE.md, Step 0 identity anchor in Recovery Chain, pre-send checklist in §14, check verification). This is the only approach that addresses the cognitive root cause rather than just adding procedural checks.

---

## Open Questions for User

None. The user's requirements are clear: investigate thoroughly and recommend the best approach. The analysis above is complete.
